<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_31b945ac-6ac4-4da7-b7df-a9c47920ae09'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1688339378" />
    <a title="Clumsy Storyteller " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21493936-clumsy-storyteller"><img alt="Clumsy Storyteller " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1542204051p2/21493936.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1688339378?book_show_action=true">Jul 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Clumsy Storyteller " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Clumsy Storyteller " href="/user/show/21493936-clumsy-storyteller">Clumsy Storyteller </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/16009267">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21493936-clumsy-storyteller?shelf=not-my-cup-of-tea">not-my-cup-of-tea</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21493936-clumsy-storyteller?shelf=the-great-shelf-of-meh">the-great-shelf-of-meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21493936-clumsy-storyteller?shelf=psychology-selfhelp">psychology-selfhelp</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1688339378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3211835625402248122">It was okay. I can't decide if my feelings on this book are mixed or simply non-existent. The concept was interesting, but it didn't bring anything new to the table, i learned nothing ! it's all about how communication is the key, how we should treat other people When they disagree with us, how we should talk less and listen more.... blah blah blah <br/><br/><b>
  <u>in three quotes, i can sum up this book: </u>
</b><br/><br/><b><blockquote>“The greatest discovery of any generation is that a human can alter his life by altering his attitude.” </blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText3211835625402248122" style="display:none">It was okay. I can't decide if my feelings on this book are mixed or simply non-existent. The concept was interesting, but it didn't bring anything new to the table, i learned nothing ! it's all about how communication is the key, how we should treat other people When they disagree with us, how we should talk less and listen more.... blah blah blah <br /><br /><b>
  <u>in three quotes, i can sum up this book: </u>
</b><br /><br /><b><blockquote>“The greatest discovery of any generation is that a human can alter his life by altering his attitude.” </blockquote>.<br /><blockquote>“If you can change your mind, you can change your life.” </blockquote><br /> <blockquote>“Whenever you're in conflict with someone, there is one factor that can make the difference between damaging your relationship and deepening it. That factor is attitude.”</blockquote>  </b><br />All quotes<b> by William James.</b><br /><br />while reading this "Self-help book'' suddenly i remembered George carlin's funny list of people who ought to be killed <br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>"List of the people who ought to be killed...Starting with these people who read self help books…why do so many people need help?! Life is not that complicated. You get up, you go to work, eat three meals, you take one good shit and you go back to bed. What’s the fucking mystery?!<br /><br />And the part I really don’t understand, if you’re looking for self help, why would you read a book, written by somebody else?! That’s not self help, that’s help!<br /><br />There’s no such a thing as self help…if you did it yourself, you didn’t need help. You did it yourself!"</b>
</blockquote><br /><br />-George Carlin<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3211835625402248122" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1558354214980615142" style="display:none">Why are those around you stupid? by Sherif Arafa, A simple, easy, and interesting book that illustrates more than one idea, and what I liked most about the book is its smoothness in clarification, and I must admit that the ending is unexpected and for my luck, I answered correctly . The only drawback is the book is the presence of topics that should be discussed more broadly, from which each idea needs to be booked separately, such as successful relationships, body language, personality styles, and the difference between men and women, and I do not mean biological difference. I mean intellectual and psychological differences. And the most important feature of the book, which encouraged me to complete it, was some wonderful words such as "I do not need to become depressed in order to solve my problems." "If I do the same thing, you will get the same result." "We may not get what we want, but we will get what you deserve." "Nothing ends Wonderfully, otherwise it would not be over."</span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mSZ3y87DcZ/ER5EqTdHuN7KIqhaNJIuDGTg/X1o6oj9GIDo2ORS7Z1VI4R1GJdlv9F/KuXTvjtFL1oZKOHu1EQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kvOTZn6zj0g5VofIbejef81K83NThwTnBrZ4E+eZ5WNN9d6biWRFsKhZ9/9mHOkni52T3KpMAbVUWMEGhdjyTQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
